***узнавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:узнавать.html>узнава́ть</a> (4256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнавать.html>узнава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uznavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to know, to recognize</li>
<li>to learn, to get to know</li>
<li>to find out, to inquire</li>
<li>to experience</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<ol><li>дознавать, разузнавать, <a href = vnd.unilang:выспрашивать.html>выспра́шивать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выпытывать.html>выпы́тывать</a></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнающий.html>узнаю́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uznajúščij</span>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:узор.html>узо́р</a> (7859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">узоръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uzorŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zretʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look, see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узор.html>узо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uzór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узор.html>узо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узор.html>узо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узор.html>узо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pattern, design, tracery</li></ol>

***узренный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:узреть.html>у́зренный</a> (15211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узреть.html>у́зренный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úzrennyj</span>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйма.html>у́йма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">újma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйма.html>у́ймы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйма.html>у́ймы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйма.html>у́йм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lots, heaps, a tremendous lot, masses</li></ol>

***уйти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a> (268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ujtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to leave, to depart, to go (away) (by foot)</li>
<li>to escape, to evade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resign, to retire</li>
<li>to be lost</li>
<li>to fail</li>
<li>to sink, to plunge</li>
<li>to be spent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a></span></b> is a Russian concrete verb. Its counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

***указ.html

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указ.html>ука́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukáz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указ.html>ука́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указ.html>ука́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указ.html>ука́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>enactment, ordinance, decree, edict, ukase

***указать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a> (1973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указывать.html>ука́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to indicate</li>
<li>to point
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо/что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukazátʹ</b> na kovó-libo/štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to point at someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give instructions, to explain</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:указка.html>ука́зка</a> (14471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указка.html>ука́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukázka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указка.html>ука́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указка.html>ука́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указка.html>ука́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pointer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orders, instructions</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:указывать.html>ука́зывать</a> (2629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***укатать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укатать.html>уката́ть</a> (25230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укатать.html>уката́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ука́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ука́тывать <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ukátyvatʹ dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the road smooth; roll a road</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to tire out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to send away</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укатить.html>укати́ть</a> (11558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклад.html>укла́д</a>(ывать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklád(yvatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладка.html>укла́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukládka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладка.html>укла́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладка.html>укла́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладка.html>укла́док</a></b>)

***укладывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a> (6538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ukládyvatʹ v postélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put to bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pack up</li>
<li>to stow, to pile, to stack</li>
<li>to arrange, to style <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of hair</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклад.html>укла́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uklád</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладка.html>укла́дка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukládka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ды<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:уложить.html>уложи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-клад-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ыва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a> (7323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukládyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уложиться.html>уложи́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улечься.html>уле́чься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pack <i>(up)</i>, to be packing <i>(up)</i>, to be packing one's things</li>
<li>to go <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сундук.html>сунду́к</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vsjó <b>ukládyvajetsja</b> v étot sundúk</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">not everything will go into the trunk</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to keep <i>(within)</i>, to confine oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фик</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukládyvatʹsja</b> v gráfik</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to be on schedule</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>за́данный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukládyvatʹsja</b> v zádannyj srok</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to meet the deadline</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́т</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">móžet li on <b>ukládyvatʹsja</b> v désjatʹ minút?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">can he manage in ten minutes?; can he confine oneself to ten minutes?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lie down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укладываться.html>укла́дываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukládyvatʹsja</b> v postélʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to go to bed</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улечься.html>уле́чься</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uléčʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укладывать.html>укла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a> (11263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inclination, rake</li>
<li>slope, declivity, gradient
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uklón</b> krýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slope of the roof</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí pod <b>uklón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">go downhill</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bias

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deviation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">heretical belief, especially relative to a prescribed form of Communism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ние</a> (28341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уклони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklonénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>evasion, avoidance; dodge</li>
<li>swerve</li>
<li>digression</li>
<li>deviation</li>
<li>deflexion</li></ol>
